msg:simply put. Come to Keketuohai, you are not short of money, and if you want to experience good accommodation conditions, environment and services, there is nothing wrong with choosing here. The housekeeper will contact you by phone and add WeChat before arrival. WeChat replies are also very timely, avoiding the fear of phone calls.

The second time I came to Keketuohai. Thinking that it is rare to come to Xinjiang, I might as well live in a better place. I think the experience is worth it. Here are a few examples.

Basically, when you enter the hotel, someone will greet you and help you with your luggage. Whether it is a snowboard bag or anything else you check in, it will be delivered to the room. This hotel that can provide such services in the entire Cocotuo Sea Town should be here.

It is difficult to take a taxi to go to other places to eat at night. Because there were too few cars and it was Chinese New Year. In fact, local prices are very low and everything is very close, but there is no car. The hotel seems to have three cars. You can contact the manager to help call a car wherever you go. It doesn't matter whether you pay or not. The key is that you have a car. If you don't have a car, try to find a way to arrange one.
If you donâ€™t want to squeeze into the bus when going to the ski resort, you can hire a taxi from your hotel and pay for pick-up. The car was warm and comfortable. You donâ€™t have to wait for the bus to make the trip.

The first day I arrived, the water was cold and small. I called the front desk to report it, and they immediately adjusted the hot water supply. A technician was sent to fix it early the next morning. The water is hot and big. The speed of door-to-door repairs is very fast.
